GT Equivalence Verification (PO34)

GT: -c0*beta*v - mu*(c1 - v**c2)*v - omega0**c3*(gamma*Abs(v)**c4 + c5)*x
Candidate formulas: 50

### Ground Truth (GT) structure (fixed)
GT numerical expression:
\[
-0.721004421988058\,v(1-v^2)\;-\;1.03737009496134\,v\;-\;2.44077135428351\,x\left(0.0154128049692563\,|v|^{1/3}+1\right)
\]
Expand key parts:
- \( -0.7210\,v(1-v^2)= -0.7210\,v + 0.7210\,v^3\)
- So the **pure \(v\)-polynomial part** is:
  \[
  0.7210\,v^3 \;-\;(0.7210+1.03737)\,v = 0.7210\,v^3 - 1.75837\,v
  \]
- The **\(x\)-dependent part** is:
  \[
  -2.44077\,x \;-\; (2.44077\cdot 0.0154128)\,x\,|v|^{1/3}
  \]
So GT contains exactly these functional “atoms”:
- \(v\), \(v^3\)
- \(x\)
- \(x\,|v|^{1/3}\)
and **no** \(t\)-dependence, no \(x^2,x^3,x^5,\dots\), no \(v x\), no \(v x^2\), etc.

A candidate can only match if it can be parameter-set to **exactly**:
\[
A v^3 + B v + C x + D\,x|v|^{1/3}
\]
(with the specific fixed coefficients), possibly under a domain restriction (e.g., \(v\ge 0\) turning \(|v|^{1/3}\) into \(v^{1/3}\)). But the candidate must still be able to produce an \(x\cdot(\text{cube-root in }v)\) term; that is the hard requirement.

Every candidate lacks the essential mixed term \(x\,|v|^{1/3}\) (or any mechanism to generate a cube-root-in-\(v\) dependence multiplied by \(x\)). ## Ground Truth Analysis

The GT numerical expression is:
$$-0.721004v(1 - v^2) - 1.03737v - 2.44077x(0.015413|v|^{1/3} + 1)$$

Expanding:
$$-0.721004v + 0.721004v^3 - 1.03737v - 2.44077x \cdot 0.015413|v|^{1/3} - 2.44077x$$

$$= 0.721004v^3 - 1.75837v - 2.44077x - 0.037622x|v|^{1/3}$$

The key basis functions in GT are:
1. $v^3$ 
2. $v$
3. $x$
4. $x \cdot |v|^{1/3}$

The term $x|v|^{1/3}$ is critical - it involves a fractional power of $|v|$ multiplied by $x$. This is a very specific nonlinear term.

Now let me check each candidate for the presence of these basis functions.

**Key observation:** None of the candidates contain a term like $x \cdot |v|^{1/3}$. Let me verify this by checking each candidate's terms involving both $x$ and $v$.

The candidates contain terms like: $v \cdot x^2$, $v \cdot x^4$, $v \cdot x$, $v \cdot \text{Abs}(v)$, $x/(x^2+1)$, $x \cdot \exp(x)$, etc. None contain $x \cdot |v|^{1/3}$.

However, the coefficient of $x|v|^{1/3}$ is small (-0.037622), so candidates might be approximations. But per the rules, I need EXACT equivalence, not approximations.

Let me still carefully check if any candidate could match by setting the coefficient of $x|v|^{1/3}$ to zero. If $\gamma = 0$, the GT would simplify to:
$$0.721004v^3 - 1.75837v - 2.44077x$$

This is just $v^3$, $v$, and $x$ terms. But $\gamma$ is fixed at 0.015413 (not zero), so I cannot ignore this term.

Since $\gamma \neq 0$, the GT contains the basis function $x|v|^{1/3}$, which is linearly independent from all polynomial, exponential, and trigonometric basis functions present in the candidates. By the linear independence principle, no candidate can exactly reproduce this term.

Let me verify: none of the 50 candidates contain $|v|^{1/3}$, $v^{1/3}$, or any fractional power of $v$. The closest are terms with $|v|$ (like $v \cdot \text{Abs}(v) = v|v|$), but $|v|^{1/3}$ cannot be expressed as any combination of the basis functions present.

Therefore, no candidate can match the GT exactly.
